MORA (WED) 01/29/1975 Palacio de los Deportes, Iztacalco, Distrito Federal [Box Y Lucha 1164, Box y Lucha 1984 (look back), https://www.facebook.com/LuchaLibreDeAyerdeHoyYSiempre/posts/835424563171947 DJ Spectro, Halcon 136, RB]Attendance: 21000
1) Atila b Villano I
## Halcon has Villano I defeating Anibal in the opener.
2) Dos Caras DQ Renato Torres
## Torres hit the ref in the third fall.
3) Cesar Valentino, El Vikingo b Rayo de Jalisco, Tinieblas
4) El Solitario, Mil Máscaras, Ray Mendoza b Canek, Dorrel Dixon, Sunny War Cloud
## Tecnicos took 1/3. Sets up War Cloud versus Mendoza for the next show.
5) Anibal  (c) DQ Rene Guajardo [NWA MIDDLE]
## A match between the last two NWA Middleweight Champions, who left the belt without being beaten. Guajardo was champ in 1974 and stripped for leaving EMLL. Anibal won the ensuing tournament, then jumped from EMLL days before this match. Anibal defended his title, though title match was likely not recognized. Guajardo weighed at 72 KG, seconded by Cesar Valentino. Anibal weighted 83 kg, seconded by Carlos Mata. Carlos Durate referee. Anibal took fall 1, Guajardo took fall 2, Guajardo knocked out Anibal with an illegal punch to the head in the third for a DQ.
&& Effective starting point LLI/UWA, though this is under the Promociones Mora banner and the UWA name does not yet exist. 345,000 peso gate, which Flores says is a record at the time.

5) Fishman b Alberto Muñoz [NWA WELTER]
## decision match for vacant NWA World Welterweight Championship. Mano Negra was forced to give up the title for leaving EMLL, but this match is happening outside of EMLL! The NWA did approve this match, but as Munoz vs Lagarde. Lagarde could not wrestle due to right leg injury (injuries for him had been a chronic issue this year.) Mano Negra appears to have not returned the (1975) current belt; Fishman is awarded the previous physical belt Negra was using earlier in his reign. Does not appear to be a national title match. Fishman took 2/3 to win, debuting Aguamala hold to win.
6) Dr. Wagner, El Halcón b Gemelo Diablo I, Gemelo Diablo II [mask]
## Diablos are Alfredo Sanchez & Jose Sanchez. Matches were set by battle royal, with these four in the final.
&& Historically listed as a UWA/Mora show, but appears to be a branded Fraternidad Santo promotion (with Flores perhaps behind the scenes.) 27,800 fans, though the KO 1151 recap believes there were close to 30,000 people there including freebees. KO 1151 has the gate as 740,000 pesos, Halcon 150 as 470,000 pesos. The actual ring was an Arena Mexico ring supplied by Chavo Lutteroth. Next show scehduled for 06/14.
